Radioligand binding assays were performed in CHO cells expressing human CCR2B and GalphaÂ±16 coupling protein. All compounds were dissolved in DMSO and assays run at a final DMSO concentration of 0.5% (v/v). [125I]-labeled human MCP-1 was purchased from PerkinElmer.
